asked the Prime Minister, Minister of Internal Ad-ministration and Deputy Minister of Defence, Public Se-curity, Law and Order :

(a) Is he aware that disappearances of persons took place during the period from the year 1986- 2000?

(b) Will he state

(i) the number of persons disappeared from each district during that period;

(ii) the number of cases that have been filed with regard to those disappearances; and

(iii) the number of cases for which the rulings have been given ?

: : INVESTMENT IN TREASURY BILLS AND TREASURY ASSETS : DELEGATIONS SENT OVERSEAS 0492 /09 6.

( ) (The Hon. Lakshman Kiriella) (1): () (i) ; (ii) ; (iii) ;

(iv) , ; ? () ? () , ? : () (i) , (ii) , (iii) , (iv) , ? () ? () , ? asked the Minister of Foreign Affairs: (a) Will he inform this House, (i) the number of delegations sent overseas from Sri Lanka to invite expatriate Sri Lankans and those employed as migrant workers to invest in treasury bills and treasury assets; (ii) the number of persons included in those dele-gations; (iii) the names and addresses of those delegates; and (iv) the amount of money spent on their airfares, lodging and other activities? (b) Will he state the amount of expenditure incurred at local and foreign level for other propaganda activities of the above programme? (c) If not, why?

( ) ( - ) (The Hon. Hussain Ahamed BhailaDeputy Ministry of Foreign Affairs) Mr. Speaker, on behalf of the Hon. Minister of Foreign Affairs, I would like to answer as follows:

2013 2014

[ ]

(a) (i) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not sent any delegations abroad to invite expatriate Sri Lankans and those employed as migrant workers to invest in Treasury Bills and Treasury assets. (ii) Does not arise. (iii) Does not arise. (iv) Does not arise. (b) Does not arise. (c) Does not arise.

asked the Minister of Community Development and Social Inequity Eradication :

(a) Will he submit to this House

(i) the amounts of money allocated to the relevant Ministry from the budgets in years 2005, 2006, 2007, 2008, and 2009; and

. ( . ) (The Hon. T. Kanagasabai) ! . NEIAP - North-East Irrigated Agriculture Project . "Re-awakening Project - . 2001 . . . . - progress, . specialist - Country Representative , , . . . , , .

. . , , . . , . , senior engineers , . . , . . . , . ! ! , ! . . , .

, - . ; . , . . , . . I would like to say a few words in English also. The NEIAP project, now called "The Re-awakening Project" funded by the World Bank is not functioning at all. I rep-resent the Batticaloa District. I am told that there is only 4 per cent progress. Now, eight months of the year have passed. The money that was allocated has not been spent. They held an interview for the selection of a Deputy Di-rector (Projects) about two or three months back but the appointment has not been made so far. There were senior engineers from the Irrigation Department working, like Mrs. Amarakoon. They are no more in service. So, it is like nobodys business; no one is interested. Today, the Minister, the Hon. Susantha Punchinilame is not here, but the Minister, the Hon. S.M. Chandrasena is here. Hon. Chandrasena, you kindly tell the Minister that something must be done in this regard. This is a sin. The money has been allocated. , . Wherever we go, they say, "No money". In this case, there is money but they are not spending it. Something must be done. That is my only request because I worked in that project for two to three years. ( ) (The Presiding Member)

Hon. Member, your time is up. . ( . ) (The Hon. T. Kanagasabai) Give me one minute, Madam Presiding Member. I have to utter a word of thanks to the Secretary, Ministry of Nation Building, Mr. W.K.K. Kumarasiri. I made a request for an allocation of some three and a half lakhs of rupees to purchase a three-wheeler for one of the col-leges in Batticaloa. The request was refused saying it is against the regulations. But, I explained to him the neces-sity to have such a vehicle. He then agreed, used his discretion and approved it. He helped me. So, I have to thank him because this is the type of government officers we want. You must make decisions. It is not a fraud or a misappropriation or anything of that sort. It is only ir-regular because it is not in accordance with the circular. But, he has made a good decision and I thank him. Thank you very much, Madam Presiding Member. ( ) (The Hon. Ranjith Aluvihare) , (2) : () (i) , ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ? () (i) ; (ii) ; (iii) ; ? () (i) ; (ii) ; ? () , ? , , :

asked the Minister of Public Administration and Home Affairs and Deputy Minister of Finance and Planning: (a) Will he inform this House

(i) the number of candidates who sat the recently held competitive examination for the recruit-ment of Grama Niladharis for the vacancies in the Wilgamuwa Divisional Secretariat Division of the Matale District;

(ii) the number of persons who passed the afore-said competitive examination; and

(iii) separately, the names of the persons who passed the aforesaid examination and the marks obtained by them? (b) Will he submit to this House

(i) out of the above - mentioned persons, the names of those who faced the interview; (ii) separately, the marks obtained by them at the interview; and (iii) the names of those who were granted appoint-ments on the result of the above - mentioned interview?

(c) Will he state

(i) the number of vacancies for Grama Niladhari that remain to be filled in this division; and

(ii) the measures that will he taken in the future to fill these vacancies?

(d) If not why?

2009 09 2247 2248

(

( () - , , ) (The Hon. (Dr.) Sarath Amunugama - Minister of Public Administration and Home Affairs and Deputy Minister of Fi-nance and Planning) 2009.09.29 1465 , 1 . . 2009.09.29 1465 1 . . Divisional Secretarys Division, Wilgamuwa in Matale District has not been included in schedule 1 of the said notification published in the gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka No. 1445 dated 29/09/09 for recruitment of Grama Niladhari since posts Grama Niladhari have not fallen vacant at that time in the above division.

Nine vacancies exist in the post of Grama Niladhari at present within the Divisional Secretarys Division Yatawatta. (d) i. In response to the case number SC (FR) 238/09 filed at the Supreme Court against the policy decision taken by the cabinet of Minister to recruit qualified applicants from Samurdhi Animators to these vacancies, an interim order has been issued to suspend new recruitments until final orders are issued on the petition. Subscriptions : The annual subscription for Official Report of Hansard is Rs. 2,178. A single copy of Hansard is available for Rs. 18.15. (Postage Rs. 2.50) Copies can be obtained by remitting in advance an annual subscription fee to the SUPERINTENDENT, GOVERNMENT PUBLICATIONS BUREAU, No. 132, Maya Avenue, Kirulapone, Colombo 5. The fee should reach him on or before November 30 each year . Late applications for subscriptions will not be accepted.
